The *Luminous Perfected* Transcendent Lords possess the golden standards for delivering the world—today, these must be enacted in the world. Looking up to the Primordial Beginning’s great compassion and prostrating below in sincere entreaty, I only pray that the sagely compassion may turn toward the teeming masses.

I wonder: might the *True Writs of the Numinous Treasure Jade Chapters* be granted for revelation in the world, to be taught to those who have not yet heard?

The ten directions: not merely the small ten directions of this realm, but the ten directions encompassing the three thousand great thousand worlds. The kalpic cycles: from kalpa to kalpa, endlessly revolving, this true governance of the world persists through every kalpa, not merely one kalpa or one era. The eight farthest reaches: the utmost distances of the three thousand great thousand worlds, not merely the eight directions visible before us. The orchid groves: fragrant jewel gardens. Heaven, Earth, and all beings possess this proper principle, and all have these groves. Yet beings, deluded, do not perceive them. The supreme perfected transcendent sages—these groves radiate their jewel-like splendor. The beneficent breeze: its grace suffuses these groves, its blessings extending to all without limit. The withered branches: beings—humans, spirits, and ghosts—who do not comprehend the proper Dharma are like deadwood. Upon hearing the true scriptures and awakening, they are like withered trees reviving. The decayed remains: beings who do not know the proper Dao, though alive, are as if dead. Upon hearing the true scriptures and transcending, even their desiccated bones are reborn. The life-giving moisture of the profound and arcane: the moisture that nourishes and revives. The *Luminous Perfected*: the Perfected Lords ennobled by the Jade Emperor. Sincere entreaty: exhausting the depths of one’s sincerity in earnest supplication to the Most Sagely. The teeming masses: those with dark hair turning white in old age, their color ashen and uncertain—hence called "teeming." It is also said: the people born of the azure heavens. It is also said: the teeming masses are the multitudes. The Numinous Treasure: the Jade Chapters, the True Writs—all explained previously. "Granted for revelation": entreating the Heavenly Worthy to transmit these scriptures, to teach them to all spirits, humans, ghosts, and beings in the Dharma-realm, delivering those who have not yet heard them. "Might they be granted for revelation to those who have not heard?"—this is a humble and tentative phrasing, not presuming to assert definitively, for fear that the Most Revered and Wondrous Dharma may not be easily transmitted. Thus, the entreaty is made first, couched in tentative language, to convey the urgency of the request and the utmost reverence.

**Chapter Six of the Divine Incantations**
Thereupon, the Primordial Heavenly Worthy stroked the armrest, raised His voice, and entered profound contemplation, gazing afar. Perceiving the time had come, He universally addressed the assembly of all true sages and saints, deliberating on yin and yang, calculating the convergences of kalpas, adjusting the reckonings of the River Source, inspecting the celestial measures, selecting the seed-people, pointing to the Supreme Non-Being, and whistling to illuminate the Nine Mysteries. Though He did not open His ears to their petitions, it was as if barriers obstructed the path to seeking the true.

At that time, the Five Elder Thearchs repeatedly posed their questions. After a long while, the Primordial Heavenly Worthy deigned to cast His gaze upon them and, with a sigh, exclaimed: "How subtle and profound! What you now inquire—is it not excellent? This is the Mystic Root of the Primordial Numinous Treasure, the true writs of the empty and spontaneous, which generate Heaven and establish Earth, open and transform the divine luminaries, bestow stability upon the Five Marchmounts, and bring peace and well-being to the nation and its people."

The numinous treasure’s profound mystery stands as the most exalted of all things, with celestial omens and numinous responses arising spontaneously. The *True Writs of the Numinous Treasure* ought to be bestowed as teachings to those yet unenlightened.

At that moment, the Primordial Heavenly Worthy caressed the jade table before Him, seated upon His precious throne, His majestic Dao-body towering and unbowed. In silent concentration of the utmost truth, He silently unfurled His boundless wisdom, gazing afar into past, present, and future. Perceiving that the time for universal deliverance had arrived, He prepared for this grand convergence, where the six conditions aligned, and all dharma-realms awaited this auspicious moment. All worlds’ celestial perfected and sagely beings deliberated upon the convergence of yin and yang, the cyclical renewal of the primordial, the reckoning of the natural rhythms of generation and transformation, the great and lesser kalpas and cosmic epochs. They adjusted the measures of the River Source’s Water Thearch, examined and recorded the celestial reckonings, selected those of good karmic seed and virtuous cultivation, pointed to the Supreme Non-Being, and chanted the ninefold mysterious verses in luminous recitation.

Mindful of the Five Elder Thearchs’ earnest pleas for the transmission of the Dharma, He knew that to withhold His compassionate assent would be as if sealing off the path to cultivating the Dao and seeking the true. At that time, the Five Elder Thearchs persisted in their supplications without cease. After a long while, the Primordial Heavenly Worthy at last unveiled His merciful countenance, His sacred gaze descending in illumination. With a sigh, He exclaimed: "How subtle and wondrous! How abysmally profound! Is not the question you now pose most excellent? This is the Mystic Root of the Primordial Numinous Treasure, the true writs of the wondrous transformations of the empty and spontaneous. They give birth to the Qian Heaven and establish the Kun Earth, open and transform all worlds’ sagely and numinous beings, stabilize the Five Marchmounts—East Tai, South Heng (also called Heng), West Hua, North Heng, and Central Song—bring peace to successive dynasties, and ensure the well-being of all dharma-realm beings.

The profound subtlety of the Numinous Treasure is most exalted among all things. Heaven manifests mysterious auspices, Earth emits felicitous omens, and all numinous responses arise naturally. *Caressing the table* refers to leaning upon the jade table of mysterious transformation, no ordinary desk. *Towering and unbowed* does not imply arrogance but describes His majestic Dao-body, the towering and immovable model of the mysterious. *Gazing afar* is sometimes mistakenly written as *thought*, but this is incorrect. *Deliberating upon yin and yang, reckoning kalpas and epochs*—the perfected and sagely are not bound by numbers. The Great Dao cannot be lightly transmitted; its timing is spontaneous. The sacred teachings do not force themselves upon the unwilling.

*Adjusting the measures of the River Source* and *recording the celestial reckonings* encompass all waters below and all heavens above, every world and all classes of beings—all are delivered. *Selecting the seed-people* does not refer solely to the virtuous. The teachings make no distinctions; when the true scriptures are expounded to the virtuous, all beings receive grace. *Pointing to the Supreme Non-Being*—the Dao’s foundation is the Great Non-Being; how can it be grasped? The Primordial Most High, in expounding these true scriptures, reveals the supreme vehicle, the true essence of the Three Teachings, the profound mystery of the empty and non-dual, enabling all who hear to attain awakening—this is what is meant by *pointing out*. *Nine Mysteries* may also be rendered as *ninefold profound mystery*, which is also acceptable.

*Gaze* refers to parting the eyes and opening the pupils, casting light upon the corners of the eyes—hence *gaze upon the corners*. It is also said that *訾* means the whites of the eyes. *Gaze* is sometimes written as *盻*, but this is incorrect.

The Primordial Most High and Perfectly Sagely One—why is the inquiry of the Five Elders of Heaven and Earth deemed virtuous? It is because they seek the true scriptures, discerning the opportune moment for their benefits, their wisdom and insight profound and subtle—hence it is called *virtuous*.

*Opening and transforming the numinous and luminous* gives rise to all immortals, gods, and buddhas.
The remaining explanations may be found above.

眦 is pronounced *zī*, or alternatively *zǐ*.

**Seven Chapters of Divine Incantations**
Now, as the reckoning of the Three Heavens unfolds and the Way of the Six Heavens operates, miscellaneous teachings emerge—there shall be thirty-six thousand kinds of Dao to dispel the doubts of those who come seeking. When this Dharma-kalpa concludes, after the Three Dragons (the three kalpas of Dragon Han) and the year of *gēngzǐ*, all杂气 shall be universally dissolved. The assemblies of the heavens shall rejoice, and Our True Dao shall then prevail.

For now, it may be entrusted, to be recorded in the Upper Celestial Repository, though it shall not yet circulate in the lower mortal world. The Mysterious Statutes bear prohibitions; it must not be recklessly transmitted.

You may proceed to the Purple Tenuity Upper Palace of the Numinous Capital, there to hearken to the celestial sounds inscribed upon the Golden Tablet, to observe the obeisance and reverence before the Divine Kings. Only then shall you be enabled to receive the celestial texts, thereby to govern in unison the heavens of the Primordial Most High.

整 is pronounced *lì*.
It is not to be written as *垫*.

When the true scriptures are transmitted, celestial portents shall manifest, numinous responses shall arise spontaneously—what age is this now? As the Three Qi of the Cinnabar Heaven renew the reckoning of qi, the thirty-six heavens shall simultaneously enact the Dao. Miscellaneous minor teachings shall emerge to open and deliver transformation, giving rise to thirty-six thousand kinds of gateways and principles to resolve the doubts of those who come seeking the Dao.

When this Dharma-kalpa concludes, after the Three Dragons (the three kalpas of Dragon Han) and the year of *gēngzǐ*, at the turning of the *Zhēnyuán* kalpa, all杂气 shall be universally dissolved. At the joyous assemblies of the heavens, Our True Dao and Orthodox Dharma shall then prevail.

For now, it may provisionally be entrusted, to be recorded in the Upper Mysterious Celestial Repository, though it shall not yet circulate in the lower dusty mortal world. The Mysterious Statutes and Celestial Laws bear prohibitions and precepts; it must not be recklessly or lightly transmitted.

You may personally proceed to the Supreme Palace of Purple Tenuity in the Numinous Capital of the Great Mystery, there to listen to the celestial sounds, to receive the solemn decrees proclaimed upon the Golden Tablet, the transmission of the ordained kalpic reckonings. Observe the obeisance and reverence before the immortals, divine emperors, celestial marshals, and heavenly kings, knowing the preciousness and profound benefits of this Dharma-treasure. Only then shall you be enabled to receive the true scriptures and celestial texts, thereby to govern in unison the heavens of the Primordial Most High’s transforming sovereignty.

整 is pronounced *lì*.
It is not to be written as *垫*.

Should one write it as *zhěng*, that too is incorrect.

The Three Heavens refer to the heavens of the Three Qi—Azure, Crimson, and Yu-Yu. The Six Heavens encompass the realms of Desire, Form, Formlessness, Light Dust, Subtle Dust, Light Defilement, and Subtle Defilement.

The Celestial Emperors, divine beings, and perfected humans expound the teachings of the Great, Middle, and Lesser Vehicles, each according to their rank in the Dao and their practice. They intersperse minor methods, offering guidance and deliverance.

There are thirty-six thousand kinds of Dao, for the human body contains thirty-six thousand spirits and qi, varying in purity and strength. Some possess right faith, others hold heterodox views; their root capacities differ, and through learning, they attain what aligns with their nature. Thus, there are the Great Vehicle and the Lesser Vehicle—hence the thirty-six thousand kinds of Dao.

This is to dispel the doubts of those who come seeking, responding to the inclinations of those who pursue the Dao. Some say it means aligning with the aspirations of seekers, each receiving and upholding what they believe in and resonate with. Those who attain enlightenment speak of it as melting like ice—this is the meaning of *shì* (释), without doubt. To write it as *zé* (择) is incorrect.

The Three Dragons refer to the beginning, middle, and end of the Dragon Han kalpa. Another account names them Dragon Han, Dragon Kang, and Dragon Zheng. When the miscellaneous qi are universally dispelled, the times grow peaceful, and demonic vapors subside.

The Celestial Assemblies are auspicious gatherings of all heavens. Another interpretation calls them joyous Dharma assemblies of the heavens.

The statutes and Celestial Laws bear natural prohibitions. Though the Dao does not select its recipients, to speak of it to the unworthy is to profane the celestial treasure and lose the weight of one’s words. Thus, the sages of the Three Teachings preached only when the time, place, and person were fitting.

The Golden Tablet and the Mysterious Register are systems for reckoning merit and transgression. To "observe obeisance before the divine kings" means to look up to the immortals and perfected ones, and to look down upon the celestial kings and divine marshals.

To "govern in unison the heavens of the Primordial Most High’s transforming sovereignty" means to oversee and administer the heavens transformed by the Primordial Most High. Another interpretation reads *shì* (示) as synonymous with *shì* (视), meaning to demonstrate the proper reverence—looking up and down—before the divine kings, thereby governing the heavens of the Primordial Most High. Both explanations are valid.

To "assemble the heavens and draw near in the imperial carriage of the Dao to the supreme heaven of the Primordial Most High" is also coherent.

**The Eight Chapters of Divine Incantations**

Thereupon, the Five Elder Thearchs, together with the perfected sages, bearing pure incense and upholding the precepts, wandered the cloud paths, summoning the ten directions. Ascending to the Supreme Clarity’s Great Mystery Jade Capital, the Hall of Cold Numinosity and Cinnabar Stair, the Supreme Palace of Purple Tenuity, they received the protocols of obeisance. Only then did they recognize the preciousness and solemnity of the celestial perfected, whose teachings are not easily heard. Returning once more before the Dao of the Primordial Most High, they consulted the rites of prohibition and precepts, humbly acknowledging their inadequacy.

After listening to the celestial sounds upon the Golden Tablet, they were then enabled to receive the true scriptures and celestial texts.

Thereupon, the Five Elder Thearchs of the Five Directions, together with the perfected sages of the heavens, clad in pure incense, upheld the precepts of the Dao, pacing the cloud thoroughfares. They guided and conveyed, lingering and wandering the cloud paths, chanting and proclaiming the decrees to the ten directions’ divine beings. Ascending to the Supreme Clarity’s Great Mystery Jade Capital, the wondrous realm of the celestial palaces, the Hall of Cold Numinosity and Cinnabar Stair, the Supreme Palace of Purple Clarity, they received the protocols of obeisance. Only then did they comprehend the solemn preciousness of the true scriptures and celestial texts, which are not easily heard.

Returning once more before the Dao of the Primordial Most High, they consulted the rites of prohibition and precepts, humbly acknowledging the limitations of their wisdom and insight.

The "pure incense" refers to the incense of true nature, the naturally pure incense of the Dao, the wondrous incense of non-action and right virtue—it is not the burning of worldly incense. To "uphold the precepts" means to maintain the solemn and majestic standards of the Mysterious Model, as if standing before the Ancestral Dao. Guarding the precepts of the Celestial Worthy, they wandered in boundless compassion, their radiant Dharma carriage traversing the cloud paths of the ten directions.

The Confucians of old said, "The light of heaven and the shadows of clouds wander together"—this is the meaning. It is not to be compared to the ceaseless coming and going of the mundane world.

To "summon the ten directions" means to issue commands with solemnity, not with whistling or laughter. The character *xiào* (啸) is read as *chì* (勅); to read it as *xiù* (秀) is incorrect. For it denotes the solemn issuance of decrees, not the act of chanting or mirth.

The "ten directions" do not refer to the Ten Numinous Treasures but to the divine hosts of the ten directions. To "ascend to the immortals and perfected ones" means to pay homage to the Primordial and receive the Dharma, silently ascending in radiant light to reverently listen to the mysterious teachings—it is not the mundane act of treading upon the steps.

The Hall of Cold Numinosity is beyond the Nine Heavens, where sound and qi do not reach, where the sun and moon cannot penetrate. The celestial light shines of itself, vast and boundless, pure and coldly solemn. The cinnabar hall gleams with the crimson radiance of great jade—hence its name.

The Supreme Palace of Purple Tenuity lies above the Purple Empyrean, within the Supreme Clarity’s Great Mystery Heaven—it is not the Purple Tenuity Palace or the Great Tenuity Palace of the mortal world’s celestial asterisms.

The protocols of obeisance have been explained previously. "Not easily heard" does not mean it is difficult to hear immediately but that it is difficult to comprehend upon hearing. Another interpretation holds that the keepers of the scriptures in the Mysterious Capital do not permit immediate hearing, so one must return once more to the presence of the Primordial Most High, ascending again to the Nine Heavens to pay homage to the Supreme Worthy and acknowledge the rites of prohibition and precepts.

*zī* (谘) has been explained previously—it means to inquire about the celestial statutes, prohibitions, precepts, and the rites of transmitting and receiving the Dharma. *jìn* (禁) refers to prohibitions; *jiè* (戒) to precepts.

"Humbly acknowledging their inadequacy" does not mean they could not uphold the prohibitions and precepts but is a gesture of humility. Though their bodies were divine and perfected, they had not yet penetrated the treasure of the true scriptures. Upon hearing them at once, their wisdom and insight were insufficient—this is precisely the reverence the Elder Thearchs of Heaven and Earth and the Five Thearchs hold for the Dao and its teachings. It is not self-limitation but an admission of unworthiness to receive them.

All things under heaven possess principle and may hear the Dao—thus the four numinous creatures each excel in their domain. Humans are the most numinous of the myriad beings, and spirits rank among the finest of the kalpic worlds. How could they be incapable of hearing the Dao?

Thus, when Yanzi daily received the teachings of the Master, he did not depart from them, appearing as if foolish, yet rejoicing in understanding. After standing firm, he said, "Though I wish to follow, there is no way." When Mañjuśrī transmitted the true essence of the Buddha’s Dharma to Śākyamuni, those who heard it were filled with awe.

This passage conveys the same meaning. Those who hold this scripture and comprehend the intent of the Elder Thearchs of Heaven and Earth and the Five Thearchs in humbly exalting its purport have thereby understood the Dao.

**The Nine Chapters of Divine Incantations**

At that time, the Heavenly Worthy, his compassionate countenance moved to instruction, opened the numinous barrier, and commanded the Five Elder Thearchs to unseal the Cavern of Yang within the Jade Palace of Primordial Clarity. They unfurled the ninefold radiance and eightfold hues of cloud-brocade wrappings to reveal the *True Writ of the Primordial Numinous Treasure’s Vermilion Script on Jade Tablets*, inscribed in gold and carved in jade—subtle, wondrous, and profoundly secret. Through it, the cosmos is governed, and the *Jade Stanzas of the Great Illuminating Perfect Mahā-Mantra of Vast Spiritual Power* were proclaimed and bestowed upon the Five Elder Thearchs.

Thereupon, the Five Elder Thearchs received the scripture with reverence, and all the divine sages of the heavens bowed their heads in homage to the Heavenly Worthy and Jade Emperor. Gazing upward, they reverently upheld the Dao’s decree and transmitted it according to the dharma.

Though the Five Elder Thearchs and the perfected sages had already humbly acknowledged their unworthiness, the Primordial Heavenly Worthy, his great compassion stirred, again instructed them with solemn admonition. The numinous barrier opened wide in transformation, and he commanded the Five Elder Thearchs to unseal the Cavern of Primordial Yang within the Jade Palace of Mystic Heaven. They unfurled the ninefold rosy clouds and eightfold luminous hues of cloud-brocade wrappings to reveal the *True Writ of the Primordial Numinous Treasure’s Vermilion Script on Jade Tablets*, inscribed in gold and carved in jade—profound, subtle, wondrous, and recondite in its secret and mysterious essence. Through it, all worlds and the cosmos are governed and transformed, and the *Jade Stanzas of the Infinite Great Illuminating Perfect Mahā-Mantra of Vast Spiritual Power* were proclaimed and bestowed upon the Five Elder Thearchs.

Thereupon, the Five Elder Thearchs received this dharma in full, and all the divine sages of the heavens bowed their heads in homage to the Heavenly Worthy and Jade Emperor. Gazing upward, they reverently upheld the decree of the Primordial Dao and transmitted it to the divine and human beings of all realms according to the golden rules of this scripture’s orthodox dharma.

*Minyu* (愍谕): "Compassionate instruction." *Min* (愍) signifies great compassion.

"Yu (谕) means 'to open and guide.' Some say it should be written as 'harmonious and joyful countenance,' but this is incorrect. The numinous barrier swings wide open. The celestial realm where the scriptures are stored—the cinnabar-spirit and mysterious gate—stands vast and unobstructed, flung open in its entirety. One interpretation holds that the sacred heart is laid bare, the mind opened to reveal sincerity. Another says the sacred eyes stream forth radiance, and the numinous barrier swings wide. Both are valid.

*Deng ming* (登命): To summon and appoint. Here, the Five Elder Thearchs are advanced and brought near to receive the command in person.

The *Jade Hall of Cavernous Yang* is the *Mystic Hall of the Nine Heavens*—a realm of boundless openness, of eternal brightness without shadow. It is not built of tiles, stone, earth, or wood, but of wondrous scenes of dark radiance, its intricate patterns of coiled script intertwining like jade inscriptions. Hence it is so called.

The *Nine Lights* have been explained earlier. The *Eight Colors* are: profound azure, profound crimson, profound yellow, profound white, profound black, verdant green, jade green, and purple-gold.

*Yun* (韫) refers to the repository where the scriptures are stored—a place where boundless dark radiance is wholly contained.

*Pi* (披) means 'to open or unfurl.' The *Cloud-Silk Satchel* is woven from the brocade of celestial clouds and mist, a natural manifestation of the Dao’s transforming light, not the handiwork of the Weaver Maid of Heaven. That which has a base is called a *satchel*, and the scriptures are inscribed within it. Its depths are unfathomable to all gods, hence the description. It is not to be compared to the cloth, silk, leather, or hides of the mortal realm.

The phrases from *Numinous Treasure* through *cosmos* have been explained earlier.

*Great Illumination*: The true scriptures of the Three Teachings are all called *Dharma-Treasures*, and wherever they reside, there is radiance. The scriptures of other teachings have limited light, but this *August Scripture* pervades the three thousand great thousand worlds, its efficacy inexhaustible even after kalpas of time. Thus it is called *Great Illumination*.

*Perfect and Complete*: The sacred heart’s compassion and salvation are boundless. Where power falls short—where there are limits or deficiencies, where the lower realms of the Northern Lu Continent cannot be transformed, nor the beings of the Heaven of Free Mastery—it cannot be called *perfect and complete*. The *August Scripture* encompasses all dharmas, unifies all vehicles, and its transformative power is measureless and inexhaustible. Though it is said that the Dao does not force itself nor clamor insistently, its transformative influence arises naturally. All beings, in their cycles of beginning and end, are ultimately transformed by the Dao. Thus it is called *perfect and complete*.

*The Jade Stanzas of the Divine Mantra*: The essential principles of all true dharma lineages, the mysterious secrets of all gods, the pivotal teachings for delivering the world. All divine powers of all teachings derive from this—none surpass its revered and peerless stature. Hence it is so called.

One reflection: When human nature awakens to the Dao, even after eons, it is not forgotten—like a satchel holding its contents without leak. The moment of awakening is like the mouth of the satchel, hence the scriptural reference to the *satchel*.

*Heavenly Worthy*: Some connect this to the preceding phrase, reading it as *paying homage to the Primordial Heavenly Worthy*. Others connect it to the following phrase, reading it as *the Jade Emperor, the Heavenly Worthy of all heavens*. The latter interpretation is preferable. The rest has been explained earlier."

Here is the translation:

---

**The Divine Incantations: Ten Chapters**

At this time, the divine incantations and decrees bestowed upon the Azure Elder of the Eastern Peace-Jewel Flower Grove, the Green Spirit and Primordial Emperor, were as follows:

**The Nine Qi of the East:**
The Primordial August Azure Heaven,
Verdant mists in layered splendor—
Within dwells the Ancient One,
Who oversees the registers and charts,
Gathers qi, and elevates the immortals.

The twenty-four secret characters of the Azure Emperor’s *Register of Transcendents* are inscribed upon the Mystic Terrace of the Nine Heavens, governing the summoning of the Nine Heavenly Thearchs and the verification of the divine immortals’ registers.

**Jupiter assists the liver;**
**Horn and Neck guard the true.**
**Root and Chamber, Heart and Tail—**
**The four seasons revolve in cycles.**
**Winnowing Basket governs the seven luminaries,**
**Aligning the Dipper and brightening its wheel.**
**Receiving qi, it seizes the false,**
**Sweeping away calamitous multitudes.**

The thirty-two secret characters of the *Star-Restraining Text* are inscribed in the Eastern Florescence Hall of the Purple Tenuity Palace, governing the summoning of stellar officials and the rectification of celestial divisions.

**The Eastern Mountain Divine Incantation**
Summons the Nine Heavens,
With vermilion-script talismanic decrees—
It commands Feng Mountain,
Binds demons and dispatches ghosts,
And none slain by it escape.
All hasten to the Wooden Palace;
Dare any delay?

The thirty-two secret characters of the *Demon-Restraining Text* are inscribed in the Mystic Numinous Lodge of Eastern Florescence, governing the subjugation of ghosts and demons and the rectification of the Nine Heavens’ qi.

**Below, it restrains the Eastern River,**
**The water spirits of the vast seas.**
**In great kalpas of flood and disaster,**
**Dragons bear their forms.**
**The Water Palace opens its paths,**
**With myriad routes and a thousand thoroughfares.**
**The Thearch’s vermilion script—**
**Wind and fire know no interval.**

The thirty-two secret characters of the *Water-Restraining Text* are inscribed upon the Cinnabar Terrace of the Jade Tower in the northeast of the Nine Heavens, governing the subjugation of the Eastern Sea’s Water Thearch, the great kalpas of flood and disaster, and the summoning of dragons and water spirits.

The true text of the *Nine Qi Numinous Treasure Jade Chapters of the East* comprises one hundred twenty characters in total. All are the spontaneous, empty, and luminous writings of the Most High, the Unsurpassed, the Great Illuminating, and Perfectly Complete Divine Incantations. It is also named the *Chapter of Cavernous Mystery for Preserving the True and Generating the Divine*, the *Eastern Mountain Divine Incantation*, and the *Eight Might Strategies of the Azure Emperor*.

By decree of the Jade Emperor, these are bestowed upon the Nine Qi Heavenly Lord, the Azure Elder of the Eastern Peace-Jewel Flower Grove, the Green Spirit and Primordial Emperor, commanding him to govern all heavens and earths of the East, the sun, moon, and stellar lodges, the sacred mountains and numinous grottoes, the water palaces and spring abodes, the lofty and venerable perfected ones, the transcendents, sages, and all numinous hosts. Wherever the talismanic decree reaches, it shall be obeyed as an imperial command.

By the Jade Emperor’s reverent observance of the Dao’s decree, the true scriptures and divine incantations are transmitted in accordance with the law—what is the meaning of this? The Five Elder Thearchs take the Eastern Thearch as their chief. The East embodies the virtue of Wood. The divine mandate bestowed upon the Azure Elder of the Eastern Peace-Jewel Flower Grove is as follows:

The six phrases from *"The Eastern Nine Qi"* to *"Upholding Qi to Ascend as Transcendents"* comprise the secret numinous writ of the Azure Thearch for delivering the world and rescuing humanity, recording the registers of transcendents—twenty-four characters inscribed upon the Primordial Terrace of the Nine Heavens, governing the summoning of the Nine Heavenly Thearchs and the verification of transcendent registers. All are the arcane, esoteric speech of the immortals, not to be minutely explicated.

The eight phrases from *"The Year Star Assists the Liver"* to *"Sweeping Away Calamitous Multitudes"* comprise the secret writ of stellar regulation—thirty-two characters inscribed within the Eastern Florescence Hall of the Purple Tenuity Palace, governing the summoning of the Stellar Lord of Wood Virtue to rectify the celestial divisions.

The eight phrases from *"The Eastern Divine Incantation"* to *"Dare There Be Delay"* comprise the secret writ for subduing the demons of the East—thirty-two characters inscribed within the Mystic Numinosity Lodge of Eastern Florescence, governing the restraint of demonic spirits and the rectification of the Nine Qi of all Eastern realms.

The eight phrases from *"Below, Commanding the Eastern Rivers"* to *"Wind and Fire Without Interval"* comprise the secret writ for the waters of the East—thirty-two characters inscribed upon the Cinnabar Terrace of the Jade Tower in the Northeast of the Nine Heavens, governing the restraint of the Eastern Sea’s Water Thearch, the great kalpic deluges, and the summoning of flood dragons and water deities.

The *True Writ of the Nine Qi Numinous Treasure Red Script Jade Chapter of the East*, totaling one hundred twenty characters, is the Great Divine Incantation of the Utmost Supreme, Great Illuminating, and Perfectly Complete, the spontaneously self-existent scripture of the Cavernous Mystery. It is also named the *Chapter of Cavernous Mystery for Preserving the True and Generating the Divine* and the *Eight Might Strategies of the Azure Emperor*. The above cannot be explicated; thus, the original text is transcribed again.

By the Jade Emperor’s decree, these are bestowed upon the Nine Qi Heavenly Lord, the Azure Elder of the Eastern Peace-Jewel Flower Grove. Commanding him to govern all heavens and earths of the East, the sun, moon, and stellar lodges, the sacred mountains and numinous grottoes, the water springs and transcendents, sages, and all numinous hosts. Wherever the talismanic decree reaches, it shall be obeyed as an imperial command. Should it be harmonized, the heavens, earth, and waters of the East, and all divine spirits, shall reverently comply with this mandate, none failing to act accordingly.

This arcane chapter is the great secret of the Azure Numinosity of heaven, earth, and all beings. Demons and ghosts lose their courage; kalpas are transcended, and calamities averted. All sages dare not disobey, and thus it eternally guards the Eastern realms.

**Eleven Chapters of Divine Incantations**
The divine incantation and mandate bestowed upon the Vermilion Elder of the Southern Flourishing Yang and Cinnabar Numinosity:

The Southern Vermilion Heaven, the Jade Hall of the Vermilion Thearch, wherein resides the Great Spirit,
Titled the Vermilion Sovereign.
Above, flames flow like smoke, the Three Qi blazing with light.
Transcendents receive their mandate, responding to the Great Yang.

The secret writ of the Vermilion Thearch for recording transcendents—thirty-two characters inscribed within the Cavernous Yang Lodge of the Nine Heavens, governing the summoning of the registers of transcendent names inscribed in gold.

Mars assists the heart; the Well and Ghost constellations guard the chambers. The Willow, Star, Spread, and Wings constellations
govern the four directions.

The Seven Mansions of the Chariot govern the celestial cycles, summoning and hastening conjunctions, rectifying the Dao’s courier paths.

The right-hand star-controlling secret writ of thirty-two characters is inscribed upon the Threefold Radiance Cinnabar Terrace, governing the summoning of stellar officials, clarifying celestial measures, and rectifying the divisions of the southern heavens.

The vermilion script commands the numinous, seizing the northern Mount Feng, binding and dispatching demonic lineages, severing evil and extirpating its roots. The talismanic teachings prosecute, exposing the origins of transgressions. The Southern Mountain divine incantation subdues the eight directions with awe. All demons are annihilated, myriad trials obliterated.

The right-hand demon-controlling secret writ of forty characters is inscribed upon the Western-Southern Yang Upright Jade Portal, governing the restraint of northern Feng, rectifying ghostly qi.

The Southern River Water Thearch, the Great Elder Dragon King—his divine incantation flows forth, universally sweeping away inauspiciousness. Floodwaters and flying calamities are stilled; dragons are summoned and flood dragons restrained. Waterways are opened, a thousand paths and ten thousand passages unobstructed. Should any dare to test this, they shall be seized and dispatched to the Fire Palace. None disobey the proclamations of the vermilion script.

The right-hand water-controlling secret writ of forty-eight characters is inscribed upon the Western-Southern Yang Upright Jade Portal, governing the seizing of the Southern River Water Thearch, the great conjunctions of cosmic cycles, the bursting forth of floodwaters in all directions, and the summoning of flood dragons and water spirits.

*The Numinous Treasure Vermilion Script Jade Chapters of the Southern Three Qi*, comprising one hundred fifty-two characters in total, are all the peerless, supreme, great luminous, perfect, and divine incantations of the self-so Void Cavern, also named *The Southern Clouds Pervading Heaven Treasure Scripture*, *The Peerless Supreme Incantation of the Nine Heavens*, and *The Vermilion Thearch’s Eightfold Might Strategems*.

The right-hand Jade Thearch’s mandate is bestowed upon the Vermilion Elder of the Southern Flourishing Yang and Cinnabar Numinosity, the Three Qi Heavenly Lord, commanding him to govern all heavens, lands, sun, moon, and stellar lodges of the southern quadrant, its sacred mountains and numinous caverns, water palaces and spring abodes, exalted sages, perfected transcendents, and all numinous powers. Wherever the talismanic mandate reaches, it is to be obeyed as a sacred edict.

The eastern writ has forever secured the eastern quadrant. What, then, is the divine incantation and mandate bestowed upon the Vermilion Elder of the Southern Flourishing Yang and Cinnabar Numinosity?

The eight lines from *The Southern Vermilion Heaven* to *responding to the Great Yang* constitute the transcendent-recording secret writ of the Vermilion Thearch, thirty-two characters inscribed within the Cavernous Yang Lodge of the Nine Heavens, governing the summoning of the registers of transcendent names inscribed in gold.

The eight lines from *Mars assists the heart* to *rectifying the Dao’s courier paths* constitute the star-controlling secret writ, thirty-two characters inscribed upon the Three Qi Cinnabar Terrace, governing the summoning of stellar officials, clarifying the celestial measures of the southern heavens, and rectifying the astrological divisions of the southern quadrant.

The ten lines from *The vermilion script commands the numinous* to *myriad trials obliterated* constitute the demon-controlling secret writ of forty characters, inscribed upon the Western-Southern Yang Upright Jade Portal, governing the restraint of northern Feng and the rectification of ghostly qi.

The twelve lines from *The Southern River Water Thearch* to *none disobey* constitute the water-controlling secret writ of forty-eight characters, inscribed upon the Western-Southern Yang Upright Jade Portal, governing the seizing of the Southern River Water Thearch, the great conjunctions of cosmic cycles, the bursting forth of floodwaters in all directions, and the summoning of flood dragons and water spirits.

The one hundred fifty-two characters of the Southern Three Qi true writ are all the supreme, luminous, perfect, and great divine incantations of the self-so Void Cavern, also named *The Southern Clouds Pervading Heaven Treasure Scripture*, *The Peerless Supreme Incantation of the Nine Heavens*, and *The Vermilion Thearch’s Eightfold Might Strategems*.

The right-hand Jade Thearch’s mandate is bestowed upon the Vermilion Elder of the Southern Flourishing Yang, the Three Qi Heavenly Lord, now commanding him to govern all heavens, lands, sun, moon, and stellar lodges of the southern quadrant, its mountains, caverns, springs, exalted transcendents, sages, and all numinous powers. Wherever the talismanic mandate reaches, it is to be obeyed as a sacred edict.

The transcendent-recording writ governs all worlds of the southern quadrant. The star-controlling writ governs all heavens of the southern quadrant. The demon-controlling writ governs all demons of the southern quadrant’s heavens, lands, and beings. The water-controlling writ governs all water thearchs and numinous entities of the southern quadrant. All the above writs governing the southern quadrant encompass all worlds of the southern direction, enduring through kalpas, eternally securing them. Even the great sages of the Three Teachings cannot transgress them.

The mysterious chapters are too sacred to be expounded. The original text is repeated to demonstrate reverence for their profound secrecy. By employing this to discipline the heart, one attains its secrets. Through devout recitation and silent contemplation, all shall witness its supreme efficacy.

**Divine Incantations, Chapter Twelve**
The divine incantation and mandate bestowed upon the Central Jade Treasure Primordial Numinous Primordial Elder Yellow Thearch:

The Central Primordial Numinous governs the Yellow Supreme Heavenly Origin, first engendering the Five Elders, the exalted Central Yellow. It seizes qi to oversee the perfected, universally leading the host of transcendents, presiding over the mysterious registers, the stellar records inscribed in jade, hastening the ascent of primordial qi, and universally proclaiming to the myriad spirits.

The right-hand transcendent-recording secret writ of the Yellow Thearch, forty characters inscribed upon the Great Mystery Jade Treasure Mysterious Astral Lodge, governs the summoning of transcendents, jade tablets, stellar destinies, and the comprehensive transcendent registers.

Saturn assists the spleen, revolving to measure the northern origin. The Demon Star, Ghost, and Ladle govern transgressions, severing evil and extirpating its roots. Demons of the mountain, the wandering, the castrated, and the auxiliary sweep away defilement and disperse miasmas. The Net and Dipper rectify the mysterious, clarifying the celestial passes. The Nine Heavens’ talismanic mandates are transmitted by the Golden Horse Couriers.

The right-hand star-controlling secret writ of forty characters is inscribed upon the Jade Terrace of the Mysterious Capital, governing the seizing of stellar officials and rectifying celestial divisions and measures.

The Central Yellow governs primordial qi, universally seizing the boundless. Saturn radiates splendor, refining the numinous palaces. It commands and seizes the Northern Thearch, blocking the gates of ghosts. Inauspiciousness is eradicated, none daring to stand before it.

The right-hand demon-controlling secret writ of thirty-two characters is inscribed upon the Jade Terrace of the Mysterious Capital, governing the seizing of the Northern Thearch, rectifying celestial qi, and restraining ghostly essences.

The Central Mountain divine incantation summons dragons to ascend the clouds, governing the confluence of the Yellow River and the nine water sources. No negligence or indulgence is permitted; good and evil are thoroughly distinguished. A thousand demons and ten thousand deceits are reported to the Thearch. None dare to test this; the Great Yang fiercely incinerates them. The vermilion script and jade characters are proclaimed universally.

The right-hand water-controlling secret writ of forty-eight characters is inscribed upon the four walls of the Mysterious Capital’s Jade Terrace, governing the waters of the Central Sea’s Water Thearch and the four springs, the reckoning of floods and surging deluges, summoning the water spirits and restraining the flood dragons.

The Central One Qi Spirit Treasure Vermilion Script Jade Chapter True Writ, comprising one hundred sixty characters in total, is the Supreme Venerable’s peerless Great Illuminating Perfect Great Divine Incantation, the spontaneously self-existent script of the Void and Cavernous, also named the *Preserving Kalpas Cavernous Clarity Nine Heavens Numinous Script*, the *Yellow Heaven Great Divine Incantation*, and the *Yellow Thearch’s Eight Mights Strategic Writ*.

The right-hand Jade Thearch’s edict and mandate bestow upon the Central Preserving Kalpas Cavernous Clarity Jade Treasure Primordial Numinous Primordial Elder Yellow Thearch, the Black Heaven Lord, authority to govern and command the Central August Earth and Heaven, the sun, moon, and stellar lodges, the numinous grottoes of famed mountains, the water palaces and spring abodes, the lofty and venerable perfected immortals, the divine transcendents and sagely hosts, and all majestic numina. Wherever the talismanic mandate reaches, it is to be obeyed as an imperial decree.

The Central Jade Treasure Primordial Numinous Primordial Elder Central Lord Yellow Thearch’s received divine incantation and edict mandate:

The Central Comprehensive Numinous Universal Proclamation to the Myriad Spirits, ten phrases of forty characters, is the *Registering Transcendents and Enrolling Immortals Yellow Thearch’s Secret Writ*, inscribed upon the Supreme Mystery Jade Treasure Mysterious Terrace, governing the summoning of divine transcendents and the jade slips of predestined fate.

The *Comprehensive Transcendent Qi*.
The *Star-Mirroring Elixir* to the *Golden Horse Post Station*, forty characters in ten phrases, is the star-controlling secret writ, inscribed upon the Mysterious Capital’s Jade Terrace, governing the seizing of stellar officials and rectifying the celestial divisions.

The *Central Yellow Comprehensive Qi* to *None Daring to Stand Before It*, eight phrases of thirty-two characters, is the demon-controlling secret writ, inscribed upon the Mysterious Capital’s Jade Terrace, governing the seizing of the Northern Thearch, rectifying celestial qi, and restraining ghostly essences.

The *Central Mountain Divine Incantation* to *Universally Proclaimed and Heard*, twelve phrases of forty-eight characters, is the water-controlling secret writ, inscribed upon the four walls of the Mysterious Capital’s Jade Terrace, governing the waters of the Central Sea’s Water Thearch and the four springs, the reckoning of floods and surging deluges, summoning the water spirits and restraining the flood dragons.

The Central True Writ of one hundred sixty characters is entirely the spontaneously self-existent script of the great divine incantation, also named the *Preserving Kalpas Cavernous Clarity Nine Heavens Numinous Script*, the *Yellow Heaven Great Divine Incantation*, and the *Yellow Thearch’s Eight Mights Strategic Writ*.

The right-hand Jade Thearch’s edict and mandate bestow upon the Central Preserving Kalpas Cavernous Clarity Jade Treasure Primordial Numinous Primordial Elder Yellow Thearch, the One Qi Heaven Lord, authority to govern and command the Central August Earth and Heaven, the sun, moon, and stars, the grottoes of mountains and springs of waters, the sagely and venerable, the hosts of transcendents, and all majestic numina. Wherever the talismanic mandate reaches, it is to be obeyed as an imperial decree.

The *Registering Transcendents and Enrolling Immortals*, the star-controlling, demon-controlling, and water-controlling secret writs dare not be loosened. This writ encompasses all the Yellow Thearch’s secrets; none can escape it. Thus, through kalpas, it eternally governs all numina of the Central Realm.

*Collected Annotations on the August Scripture*, Scroll Five concludes.

---

*Collected Annotations on the August Scripture*, Scroll Six

Successor Han Fifty-First Celestial Master, Great Perfected Zhang Guoxiao, collated.
Former Principal Graduate, Recluse Beyond the Red Dust of Jishui, Jiangxi, Luo Hongxian, reviewed.
Xiaozhaochen of Jinan, Shandong, Zhou Xuanzhen, compiled.

**Thirteenth Chapter of the Divine Incantations: The Western Seven Treasures Golden Gate Radiant Numinous August Elder White Thearch’s Received Divine Incantation and Edict Mandate**

The Western Plain Heaven, the White Thearch’s Seven Gates,
Golden Numinous Radiance gleams, the Great Hua diffuses its mist.
White stones towering, the seven qi suffuse and swirl.
Above, the Primordial Birth, the August Elder Great Spirit,
Oversees the lung qi, governs the nine heavens’ reckoning,
Verifies and establishes the celestial registers, commands and summons the lofty transcendents.

The right-hand *Registering Transcendents and Enrolling Immortals White Thearch’s Secret Writ* of forty-eight characters is inscribed upon the northern pavilion of the Nine Heavens Plain Numinous Palace, governing the summoning of transcendent qi and the elevation of the immortal Dao.

The Great White verifies the lungs; Kui and Lou guard the hun-souls.
Stomach, Pleiades, Net, and Turtle Beak.

**Governor of the Seven Passes.**
Participating in the Dipper’s Handle, receiving talismans from the Northern Origin.
The right-hand *Star-Controlling Secret Writ* of twenty-four characters is inscribed upon the Golden Pass’s Mystic Window, governing the summoning of the White Thearch’s stellar officials and rectifying the celestial reckonings.

Red-script jade characters, the Nine Heavens’ orthodox writ,
Drawing in the ten thousand qi, universally returning to the Thearch-Lord.

The right-hand *Demon-Controlling Secret Writ* of sixteen characters is inscribed within the Nine Heavens’ Golden Pass Hall to subdue the qi of the Six Heavens’ demons.

The Western Mountains’ divine incantation, Eight Might and Seven Assistants.
Talismanic water ascends the dragon, summoning mountains and dispatching clouds.
Wherever verification and registration occur, all converge at the Thearch’s Gate,
Aiding and guarding the lofty perfected, severing and extinguishing the roots of evil.
Should any inauspiciousness arise, it is intercepted by the Golden Pass.
Red-script talismanic commands, transmitted by wind and water couriers.

The right-hand *Water-Controlling Secret Writ* of forty-eight characters is inscribed within the Nine Heavens’ Golden Pass’s Three Charts Hall, governing the summoning of the Western Sea’s Water Thearch and all malevolent and venomous spirits within the waters, calling forth cloud-dragons to prevent floods and droughts.

The *Numinous Treasure Red-Script Jade Chapter True Writ* of the Seven Qi of the West, totaling one hundred thirty-six characters, is the peerless, supremely radiant, perfectly complete great divine incantation of the Most High, the spontaneously self-existent writ of the Void Cavern. It is also called the *Golden Perfected Treasure Luminance Cavern Subtlety Chapter*, the *Western Mountains’ Divine Incantation*, and the *White Thearch’s Eight Might Dragon-Summoning Writ*.

The right-hand *Jade Thearch’s Decree* is bestowed upon the Seven Qi Heavenly Lord of the Western Seven Treasures Golden Gate, August Elder White Thearch, commanding him to govern all heavens and earths of the West, the sun, moon, and stellar lodges, the numinous grottoes of famed mountains, the palaces of water bureaus and springs, the lofty perfected and exalted worthies, the host of perfected transcendents and sages, and all numinous powers. Wherever the talismanic command reaches, it is to be obeyed as a decree.

The *Western Seven Treasures Golden Gate August Elder White Thearch’s Received Divine Incantation Decree*:
The twelve phrases of forty-eight characters from *Western Plain Heaven* to *governing the summoning of transcendent qi* are the *Registering Transcendents and Enrolling Immortals White Thearch’s Secret Writ*, inscribed upon the northern pavilion of the Nine Heavens’ Plain Numinous Palace to summon transcendent qi and elevate the immortal Dao.

The six phrases of twenty-four characters from *Great White verifies the lungs* to *receiving talismans from the Northern Origin* are inscribed upon the Mystic Window of the Golden Palace as the *Star-Controlling Secret Writ*, governing the summoning of the White Thearch’s stellar officials and rectifying the celestial reckonings.

The four phrases of sixteen characters from *Red-script jade characters* to *universally announcing to the Thearch-Lord* are inscribed within the Nine Heavens’ Golden Palace’s Three Charts Hall as the *Demon-Controlling Secret Writ* to subdue the qi of the Six Heavens’ demons.

The twelve phrases of forty-eight characters from *Western Mountains’ divine incantation* to *wind and fire couriers* are the *Water-Controlling Secret Writ*, inscribed within the Nine Heavens’ Golden Palace’s Three Charts Hall to govern the summoning of the Western Sea’s Water Thearch and all malevolent and venomous spirits within the waters, calling forth cloud-dragons to prevent floods and droughts.

The *True Writ of the Seven Qi of the West*, totaling one hundred thirty-six characters, is the great divine incantation of the Most High, also called the *Golden Perfected Treasure Luminance Cavern Subtlety Chapter*, the *Western Mountains’ Divine Incantation*, and the *White Thearch’s Eight Might Dragon-Summoning Writ*.

The right-hand *Jade Thearch’s Decree* is bestowed upon the Seven Qi Heavenly Lord of the Western Seven Treasures Golden Gate, August Elder White Thearch, commanding him to govern all heavens and earths of the West, the stellar lodges, mountain grottoes and water springs, the host of perfected transcendents and sages, and all numinous powers. Wherever the talismanic command reaches, it is to be obeyed as a decree.

The *Registering Transcendents and Enrolling Immortals*, *Star-Controlling*, *Demon-Controlling*, and *Water-Controlling* writs encompass all the secrets of the West; they dare not be openly expounded.
*Summoning mountains and dispatching clouds* refers to the summoning of the mountains’ mysterious numinous true qi. Those who write it as *止* (to stop) are incorrect.

**Fourteen Incantation Chapters**
The *Divine Incantation Decree Received by the August Elder Black Thearch of the Five Qi of the Northern Cavernous Yin, Solitary Desolation, Utter Stillness*:
The Northern Mysterious Heaven, the Five Qi meander.
Within it, the Black Thearch, the Dual August Ones of the Grand Tenuity,
Oversee talismanic commands.
Transcendents refine the Eight Might, clad in azure skirts and feathered headdresses,
Dragon-script and phoenix robes.
Raised by the Thearch, they are commanded to ascend the jade steps.

The Forty-Character Secret Writs of the Black Thearch for Delivering Humans and Registering Transcendents shall be inscribed within the Northern Pavilion of the Boundless Mysterious Origin, the Purple Tenuity Palace of Utmost Solitude. They govern the summoning of all Perfected Ones and the divine transcendents’ talismanic registers.

The Northern Culmen aids the kidneys; the Dipper and Ox guard the gates.
The Maiden, Void, and Rooftop open the Four Vastnesses.
The Wall commands the Seven Stars, warding off misfortune and correcting wrongs.
They dispel calamities, sweep away defilements, illuminate the Dao, and activate radiance.

The Thirty-Two-Character Secret Writs for Controlling Stars shall be inscribed within the Northern Mysterious Heart of the Celestial Pivot, the Dark Dipper. They govern the subjugation of the stellar officials of the North and the rectification of celestial qi.

The Northern Mountain Incantation rouses yang to summon thunder.
The Flowing Bells blaze and scatter; the Heavenly Apes shake their might.
The legions of the Northern Feng all perish, myriad demons crushed.

The Twenty-Four-Character Secret Writs for Controlling Demons shall be inscribed upon the Mysterious Terrace of the Northern Cavernous Yin, Utmost Solitude. They govern the subjugation of the Celestial Demons of the Northern Thearch and the suppression of all malevolent spirits and myriad ghosts.

The Nine Rivers pour forth; the Bird Mother and her flock take flight.
The flood dragons clear the paths; the watery thoroughfares open wide.
The Vermilion Script and Jade Writs speed like dragons borne on the wind.

The Twenty-Four-Character Secret Writs for Controlling Water shall be inscribed upon the Primordial Terrace of the Northern Cavernous Yin, Utmost Solitude. They govern the subjugation of the Water Thearchs of the Nine Seas, the control of the myriad spirits within the waters, and the summoning of flood dragons to raise clouds and command rain.

The Vermilion Writs of the Five Qi Numinous Treasure of the North, totaling one hundred and twenty characters, are all the Supreme, Peerless, Great Illuminating, Perfect, and Complete Divine Incantations—the spontaneously generated writs of the Hollow Cavern. They are also called the *Life-Sustaining Purple Tenuity Primordial Spirit’s True Treasure Luminous Writs*, the *Northern Mountain Incantation*, or the *Black Thearch’s Eight Might Celestial Control Writs*.

The Jade Thearch’s Decree is bestowed upon the Five Qi Heavenly Lords of the Northern Cavernous Yin, Utmost Solitude, the Primordial Elder Black Thearch, commanding them to govern all heavens and earths of the North, the sun, moon, and stellar lodges, the sacred mountains and numinous caverns, the water palaces and spring abodes, the lofty sages and exalted worthies, the Perfected Transcendents and divine multitudes, and all numinous powers. Wherever the talismanic commands reach, they shall be obeyed as decreed.

The Divine Incantation Decree Received by the August Elder Black Thearch of the Five Qi of the Northern Cavernous Yin, Utmost Solitude:

The forty characters from *The Northern Mysterious Heaven* to *ascend the jade steps* are the Secret Writs of the Black Thearch for Delivering Humans and Registering Transcendents. Inscribed upon the Northern Pavilion of the Mysterious Strider, they govern the summoning of all Perfected Ones and the divine transcendents’ talismanic registers.

The thirty-two characters from *The Northern Culmen aids the kidneys* to *activate radiance* are the Secret Writs for Controlling Stars. Inscribed within the Northern Mysterious Heart of the Celestial Pivot, the Dark Dipper, they govern the subjugation of the stellar officials of the North and the rectification of celestial qi.

The twenty-four characters from *The Northern Mountain Incantation* to *myriad demons crushed* are the Secret Writs for Controlling Demons. Inscribed upon the Mysterious Terrace of the Northern Cavernous Yin, Utmost Solitude, they govern the subjugation of the Celestial Demons of the Northern Thearch and the suppression of all malevolent spirits and myriad ghosts.

The twenty-four characters from *The Nine Rivers pour forth* to *dragons borne on the wind* are the Secret Writs for Controlling Water. Inscribed upon the Primordial Terrace of the Northern Cavernous Yin, Utmost Solitude, they govern the subjugation of the Water Thearch of the Northern Sea, the control of the myriad spirits within the waters, and the summoning of flood dragons to raise clouds and command rain.

The True Writs of the Five Qi of the North, totaling one hundred and twenty characters, are all the Supreme Divine Incantations. They are also called the *Life-Sustaining Purple Tenuity Primordial Spirit’s True Treasure Luminous Writs*, the *Northern Mountain Incantation*, or the *Black Thearch’s Eight Might Celestial Control Writs*.

The Jade Thearch’s Decree is bestowed upon the Five Qi Heavenly Lords of the Northern Primordial Elder Black Thearch, commanding them to govern all heavens, earths, sun, moon, and stars of the North, the mountains, caverns, waters, and springs, the Perfected Transcendents and divine multitudes, and all numinous powers. Wherever the talismanic commands reach, they shall be obeyed as decreed.

The Writs for Delivering Humans and Registering Transcendents, for Controlling Stars, Demons, and Water, encompass all the secrets of the Northern Mystery. Thus, none may ever transgress them.

Upon bestowing the True Writs of the Five Directions and Five Thearchs, they eternally guard all worlds. The Three Teachings and myriad beings cannot escape their sway; they endure for eternal kalpas, wondrously existing in the void, their mysteries unfathomable. Profound beyond profundity, their divinity is divine indeed.

The five qi of my own body fully embody this principle. Those of resolve and understanding, who penetrate the essence of life and destiny and grasp the source of the myriad dharmas, cannot be contravened by principles or numerology. The True Scripture is ever within me; the efficacy and transformation of the divine incantations reside herein.

**Fifteen Incantation Chapters**
The Dao speaks: These Great Divine Incantations are the wondrous words of the Primordial Commencement, the true decrees of the Jade Thearch, the numinous writs spontaneously generated by the Supreme Purity, the mysterious writs born at the inception of the Nine Heavens, the numinous chapters of the Hollow Cavern, the secret utterances of the loftiest sages, the exalted canon of the Jade Capital. They establish heaven and earth, unfold the myriad transformations, pacify spirits and secure the numinous, engender and complete the multitudes, rectify and govern the cosmic cycles, and preserve the heavens’ eternal endurance. Above, they control the mechanisms of heaven; at the center, they regulate the five numina; below, they command the earthly deities. They command the sources of rivers, mobilize yin and yang, summon spirits and dispatch transcendents—this is the wondrous subtlety of the utmost truth.

Moreover, their divine responses arise spontaneously, causing the heavens to soar and clear, the earth to stand firm and secure, and the Five Marchmounts to be safeguarded, wherein the myriad beings abide.

Why are the divine transformations of the Five Directions’ incantations boundless?
The Dao speaks: These Great Divine Incantations are the wondrous words of the Most Supreme Primordial Commencement Thearch, the precious decrees of the Most True Jade Thearch, the numinous writs spontaneously generated by the Supreme Purity Mysterious Capital, the mysterious celestial writs born at the inception of the Nine Heavens’ immortal realms, the numinous chapters of the Great Void and Hollow Cavern, the secret utterances of the Most Supreme and Peerless Loftiest Sages, the most exalted dharma canon of the Purple Ultimate Jade Capital. Above, they perfect the myriad heavens; below, they establish the myriad earths. They unfold the wondrous transformations of the myriad existences, unify the spirits, and secure the myriad numina. In their singular generation and completion, they govern the billions of beings, uphold and assist the secrets of cosmic cycles and deliverance, and preserve the eternal endurance of the heavens. Above, they control the great generative mechanisms of the celestial canopy; at the center, they regulate the Five Directions’ five numina; below, they command the earthly deities. They command all water palaces and river sources, transform and mobilize yin and yang, and summon all spirits and transcendents. These Great Divine Incantations are the wondrous writs of the utmost truth, whose divine transformations and wondrous responses arise solely from spontaneity.

Above, they abide in Heaven, attaining the One to achieve purity—lofty, luminous, and enduring, thus establishing Heaven’s towering clarity. Below, they abide in Earth, attaining the One to achieve tranquility—vast, profound, and enduring, thus establishing Earth’s steadfast constancy. They eternally pacify and secure the Five Peaks and renowned mountains, ensuring the perpetual existence of all myriad beings and their kinds.

The Dao declares: It is the Five Venerable Thearchs who expound the Dao and offer praises, hence the attribution to the Primordial Jade Sovereign—this is not the Primordial’s self-praise. The wondrous and numinous scriptures mentioned here have all been explained previously.

The *Nine Heavens’ Primordial Mysterious Writs* are called "writs" as they are inscribed by hand. The *True Scripture of the Jade Sovereign* is formless and soundless, its radiant light and wondrous tones pervading the ten directions and the entire Dharma Realm, enduring through kalpas without decay. It is not something that can be inscribed by hand—all is the spontaneous script; not something that can be transmitted by speech—all is the wondrousness of mind-to-mind transmission. Sought in the beginningless, it exists prior to the formless in the Great Void, hence it is called the *Nine Heavens’ Primordial Mysterious Writs*.

The *Venerable Canon of the Jade Palace*—the "palace" is where the Son of Heaven resides. The Primordial is the supreme honor of all teachings, dwelling in the Sacred Realm of Jade Purity, whose mysterious transformations are inexhaustible, hence it is called the *Jade Palace*. In expounding this true scripture, none of the teachings’ scriptures compare; none of the sages or spirits dare defy it. The celestial statutes and golden registers treasure it most profoundly; the saints of the ten directions guard it most strictly, hence it is called the *Venerable Canon*.

To "pacify the spirits" is to command all spirits to refrain from displaying their numinous powers, remaining serene and non-active. To "secure the numina" is to command all numina to conceal their spiritual resonance, restraining their majestic efficacy. To "uphold and assist the cycles of deliverance" is to govern the kalpas from beginning to end throughout the Dharma Realm, holding the turning of kalpas and the boundless deliverance, ensuring their cyclical perpetuity without decline or wavering.

To "command the earthly deities" is to issue decrees and edicts—this is not the "whip" of coercion. To "mobilize and employ yin and yang" means that the Dao truly governs their alternation, hence it is called "mobilizing and employing"—this does not refer to commanding yin ghosts or yang spirits. To "summon the spirits" is to gather and call forth all spirits. To "employ the transcendents"—though transcendents are the guests of the Thearch, why speak of "employing" them? When the Primordial expounded this scripture, it became the true essence of the Three Teachings, and all spirits reverently complied, hence it is called "employing the transcendents."

Heaven and Earth may perish, and the myriad kinds may come to an end—how then can it be said that all beings endure? From kalpa to kalpa, generation after generation is inexhaustible, all relying on the Great Dao, hence it is said that all beings endure.

**The Sixteen Chapters of the Divine Incantations**
were once bestowed by the Jade Sovereign upon the Five Venerable Thearchs. At that time, the Five Thearchs knelt and reverently held the chapters, secretly inscribing them in the numinous capital. The Heavenly Perfected Sovereign once transcribed the text, enshrining it in the Supreme Clarity’s True Realm, the Great Mystery’s Jade Capital, the Cold Numinous Cinnabar Hall, and the Purple Tenuity’s Upper Palace. Through countless kalpas and cosmic cycles, the text has preserved the celestial root, remaining uncorrupted and undiminished, evolving in tandem with the turning of kalpas.

This Great Divine Incantation, when confounded, remains unstained; when defiled, grows ever purer. When destroyed, it does not perish; when extinguished, it shines with utmost clarity. The scripture of the Great Existence is revered by the Heavenly Perfected, its true name resplendent with celestial radiance. The Thearch’s chart is inscribed upon golden tablets, illuminating future generations. This scripture is profoundly hidden and secret—ordinary beings cannot glimpse or hear of it. Those who attain this Dao preserve the eternal endurance of the myriad qi. Through diligent practice and devotion, they attain transcendence and ascend to pay homage to the Most Honored Thearch.

To "kneel and hold" is to prostrate and reverently cradle the treasure chapters. The scripture exists in Heaven as a mysterious text, not a worldly one—how then can it be "held by hand"? The celestial spirits bow and hold it in utmost reverence. To "secretly inscribe" is to praise and transcribe it. The Heavenly Perfected Sovereign’s transcription of the scripture consists of celestial radiance and heavenly writ, golden and jade characters forming wondrous texts a *zhang* in length.

The *True Realm of Supreme Clarity* is the abode of the Numinous Treasure. The scripture was originally expounded by the Primordial Heavenly Worthy and transmitted by the Numinous Treasure, hence it is called the *True Realm of Supreme Clarity*. That "its text preserves the celestial root" means the principle of the scripture endures through kalpas without decay—it preserves the eternal constancy of the celestial mystery. Some interpret this as preserving the root of Heaven to ensure its perpetuity, but this is incorrect. After the cosmic cycles, Heaven cannot endure eternally, so it cannot refer to the root of Heaven. "Evolving in tandem with the turning of kalpas" means it endures through kalpa after kalpa.

"When confounded, it remains unstained" means that even when mixed with heterodox teachings, the true Dao persists and cannot taint this scripture. "When defiled, it grows ever purer" means that those who profane this scripture are punished by Heaven, revealing its ever-greater sanctity and purity. "When destroyed, it does not perish" means that even when foolish and perverse beings slander and destroy this scripture, it remains indestructible. "When extinguished, it shines with utmost clarity" means that in an age without the Dao, those who seek to extinguish this scripture will only cause its teachings to spread widely, revealing its ever-greater luminosity.

The "scripture of the Great Existence" endures through kalpas, present everywhere—it is not an ordinary phenomenon but a wondrous existence, hence it is called the *Great Existence*. Some interpret this as the scripture of the *Great Existence* and the *Court*, but this is overly restrictive.

Revealing the future lives, it speaks not of one person’s rebirth but of the myriad lives to come. Those who cannot glimpse or hear of it are not the utmost sages, for common folk merely recite its words. Demons dare not peer into it, and the benighted cannot comprehend it. Those who grasp the principles within this scripture preserve the eternal flow of my myriad *qi*, diligently cultivating and revering it, and thus ascend to immortality, paying homage to the Supreme Emperor. Some say it is homage to the Five Elder Lords, but this is overly restrictive. Another interpretation holds that it preserves the eternal *qi* of the myriad transformations, which is also valid. This speaks to the scripture’s manifest efficacy.

**Chapter Three: The Jade Emperor’s Virtues and Powers**
*Continuation of the "Virtues and Powers" Chapter, Eighteenth Section Following the Previous Seventeen*

At that time, the Jade Void Emperor addressed the Heavenly Worthy, saying: "I earnestly wish for your compassion to universally benefit the Four Assemblies, Lord Śakra, the Four Brahmā Heavenly Kings, all the devas, all the immortals, and all future beings, as well as those who uphold this scripture, by expounding its beneficial matters."

At that time, the Heavenly Worthy spoke to the Jade Void Emperor: "Excellent indeed is this question! How good it is! You, moved by compassion, take pity on sentient beings and thus inquire of me. You should resume your seat, and I shall proclaim and expound."

When the Jade Emperor bestowed this scripture upon the Five Elder Lords, the Heavenly Emperor of the Jade Void Heaven ascended to address the Great Heavenly Worthy, Master of Scriptures and Teachings: "I earnestly wish for your utmost sagely compassion to universally benefit the Four Assemblies of the world, all the deva-kings such as Lord Śakra, the Four Brahmā Heavenly Kings above the Three Realms, all the devas, all ranks of immortals, all future beings, and those who uphold this true scripture, by expounding its beneficial matters."

At that time, the Great Heavenly Worthy, Master of Scriptures, addressed the Jade Void Emperor: "How joyous indeed is this question! How good it is! You, moved by a heart of compassion, take pity on the beings of the world and thus inquire of me. You should resume your seat, and I shall proclaim and expound the scripture’s meaning."

When the Heavenly Worthy refers to the Primordial Beginning, it is not the Jade Emperor. The Four Assemblies have been explained previously. Lord Śakra is the lord of the devas, including all buddhas and bodhisattvas of the Buddhist teachings. Some hold that all heavenly lords are called Śakra, which is also correct. If one takes *Śakra* to mean the lord of the Heaven of the Thirty-Three, this is a misconception of the Buddhist tradition. The scriptures do not mistakenly refer to the lord of heaven as the Jade Emperor, for the Jade Emperor is the ancestor of the myriad heavens, not merely the lord of a single heaven. The Buddhist scriptures state that Brahmā and Śakra present auspicious signs, speaking of the ancestral figures of heaven and buddhahood, not presuming to mention the Jade Emperor. Monks who indulge in private misinterpretations commit a grave error. Thus, this is mentioned here as well.

The Four Brahmā Heavenly Kings are the great Brahmā kings above the Three Realms, not the kings of the lower heavens of the Desire Realm. To speak of Brahmā Heaven is to encompass the upper realms. The *zhongmin* heavens and their denizens are not mentioned, for above the *zhongmin* are the perfected great immortals who naturally accord with this scripture, hence they are not included. "All the devas" and "all the immortals" refer to all the heavenly lords, divine beings, and people, as well as all ranks of immortals below Brahmā Heaven.

The question of beneficial matters: The Great Dao does not speak of efficacy, so why does the Jade Void Emperor request an explanation of its benefits? The Great Dao is the ancestor of heaven, earth, and all beings, inherently possessing true benefits and natural advantages for humanity. Those among the Four Assemblies of heaven and earth who do not know this scripture are ignorant of its meaning, dare not believe in it, and thus slight the great Dharma, misleading themselves. The Great Dao, in its benevolent compassion, cannot bear the world’s delusion and thus speaks of benefits to deliver beings. How is it that the foolish and deluded still claim this scripture consists of subtle words and abstruse theories, of what benefit is it to people? Do they not know that this scripture gives rise to heaven, earth, and all beings, and cannot be separated from for even a moment? Everywhere, everyone should recite and uphold it, passing it down through kalpas, for it brings great benefits naturally, not merely to entice people with effects.

"How good it is!" is not a question but an affirmation of the excellence of the inquiry. "I" refers to the Primordial Beginning speaking of himself. "You" refers to the Primordial Beginning addressing the Jade Void Emperor. "Resume your seat" instructs the Jade Void Emperor to return to his seat for listening to the scripture. "I" is also the Primordial Beginning referring to himself. "Proclaim and expound" means to broadly disseminate as proclamation and to explain as discourse.

*Fan* (梵) is pronounced *fu* (扶), not mistakenly as *fan* (梵). This expresses the sincerity of the request for the scripture and the heart of universal benefit.

*Continuation of the "Virtues and Powers" Chapter, Eighteenth Section*

The Heavenly Worthy said: "If in the Three Realms, the ten directions, and the boundless lands, warfare erupts, pestilence spreads, floods, droughts, locusts, or dire calamities and famines arise, then the king and his ministers should arouse compassion and, for the sake of their people, issue decrees throughout the land, ordering the governors of provinces, counties, and towns to command all Daoist followers to purify and adorn their oratories. There, they shall hold grand fasts and jiao rites, perform the six-hour circumambulation, and recite this scripture. Thus, the land shall attain peace, the five grains shall ripen abundantly, and the people shall live in tranquility."

The Primordial Heavenly Worthy, having instructed the Jade Void Emperor to resume his seat and listen to the scripture, then said: "If in the Three Realms of heaven, earth, and humanity, the ten directions of the four cardinal and four intermediate directions, and the boundless lands, warfare erupts and weapons clash, or celestial disasters spread and pestilence rages, or years of scarcity bring floods, droughts, locusts, dire calamities, and famine, then the king and his ministers should arouse compassion for their people and issue decrees throughout the land. The governors of provinces, counties, and towns shall command all Daoist followers to purify and adorn their oratories. There, they shall hold grand fasts and jiao rites, perform the six-hour circumambulation, and recite this true scripture. Thus, the land shall attain peace, the five grains shall ripen abundantly, and the people shall live in tranquility."

Some say that the Three Realms cannot include heaven, fearing conflict with the term *weapons*. Yet even heavenly demons contend with the lords of the heavens, engaging in battles within their respective domains. Thus, the Three Realms indeed encompass heaven, earth, and humanity."

When warfare arises, it refers only to conflicts breaking out in various regions, with mutual hostilities—it does not mean that both "weapons" and "halberds" emerge simultaneously. Swords, spears, and the like are all weapons, including halberds and polearms. Thus, it is incorrect to speak of their concurrent emergence. Some say that "soldiers rise as men, and men and halberds arise together," but this is also not the proper meaning.

When pestilential qi spreads widely, the heavenly Dao remains in its constant state, while calamities are called "changes." The rampant spread of pestilential qi is a time of plague, which is also an inauspicious anomaly. This scripture dispels and averts such afflictions.

Floods and droughts, locusts and insects—overflowing waters, parched lands, various pests harming crops, and swarms of locusts damaging harvests—are all inauspicious anomalies. Dire calamities and famine occur when the year’s harvest fails and the people and creatures are unsettled, making it "dire." The abnormal is called "calamity." Grain failing to ripen is "famine," while vegetables failing to ripen is "dearth." All these are inauspicious anomalies.

黎 refers to the black-haired people; 庶, to the common folk. 遍勑 is synonymous with 遍敕. 州县镇宰 may refer to the officials governing prefectures, counties, and towns who oversee the people, or to military commanders in garrisons. Some say it refers to grand officials like governors and viceroys. All these interpretations are valid.

Thus, "the king and his ministers" refers to the kings and ministers of such places.

The Daoist lineages—Quanzhen, Zhengyi, Qingwei, Lingbao, and other schools—maintain purity and solemnity, both inwardly and outwardly, with body and mind undivided. Their altars and vestments are impeccably ordered, their reverence and dignity unwavering from beginning to end. Such is their purity and solemnity.

*Guan* (觀) means "to observe." Where the spirit resides, onlookers are moved to reverence—this is truly a grand spectacle. Hence, it is called *guan*.

When grand *zhai* (斋) and *jiao* (醮) rites are conducted, inner and outer realms are aligned, the will of the assembly is unified, and what was discordant is harmonized—this is *zhai*. To beseech and give thanks to the deities, repaying Heaven and Earth, aligning one’s virtue with the divine, and invoking blessings according to ritual—this is *jiao*.

The "six periods of Dao-recitation" do not refer to the modern practice of processional recitation along roads, but rather to invoking the deities, reciting scriptures, and chanting the Dao according to ritual. Some say that of the twelve hours of day and night, odd hours are for activity and even hours for stillness. The "six periods" correspond to *zi* (子), *yin* (寅), *chen* (辰), *wu* (午), *shen* (申), and *xu* (戌). Others say they span from *zi* to *si* (巳), or refer to the six daylight hours. All interpretations are valid.

When scriptures are recited with the heart in union with the Dao, holding fast to the true scripture, the land knows no hardship, and peace prevails. The five grains—rice, millet, sorghum, beans, and wheat—all ripen in abundance, and the black-haired people of every land and realm are spared from disaster and suffering, forever dwelling in tranquility and joy.

**Chapter on Meritorious Virtues (Continuation of Chapter Nineteen)**
