**Seventh,** deliverance from water and fire calamities;
**Eighth,** the silent dissolution of misfortunes;
**Ninth,** auspicious dreams at night;
**Tenth,** immunity from illness;
**Eleventh,** wisdom and keen intelligence;
**Twelfth,** delight in the sight of others;
**Thirteenth,** abundance in clothing and food;
**Fourteenth,** honor and nobility for descendants—let them be virtuous and pure, free from baseness, ignominy, or early death, and all shall be well;
**Fifteenth,** joy among the six relations;
**Sixteenth,** harmony within the clan;
**Seventeenth,** eradication of the three evil retributions;
**Eighteenth,** transformation of a woman’s body into a man’s;
**Nineteenth,** a dignified and majestic appearance;
**Twentieth,** appointment as a great minister of the state;
**Twenty-first,** birth as the son of an emperor;
**Twenty-second,** reverence and admiration from ghosts and spirits;
**Twenty-third,** attainment of knowledge of past lives—all karmic obstructions dissolved, and life’s path made smooth;
**Twenty-fourth,** protection and mindfulness from all deities;
**Twenty-fifth,** the nine clans receiving blessings—the nine clans being: high ancestors, great-grandparents, grandparents, parents, oneself, children, grandchildren, great-grandchildren, and great-great-grandchildren; or, alternatively, three clans on the father’s side, three on the mother’s, and three on the wife’s;
**Twenty-sixth,** longevity in the world;
**Twenty-seventh,** all sentient beings relying on one’s virtuous merit;
**Twenty-eighth,** the demon kings safeguarding and welcoming;
**Twenty-ninth,** transcending the three realms of desire, form, and formlessness in succession;
**Thirtieth,** ascension in broad daylight.

Though immortals ascend in varied ways—not all necessarily rising bodily in daylight—those who attain this state become as vast as the great void, their spirits roaming the Jade Capital: this is ascension in broad daylight.

Devout reverence for this scripture and the August Lord yields such merits, yet one must first utterly renounce secret desires, seek no verification of effects, and persist without interruption. When the heart aligns with heaven, efficacy follows; even if it does not, no harm comes from doing good. Should one covet verification, they have not truly transmitted the scripture of the August Lord. Let the reader take heed.

**Chapter Thirty-Five: Further Manifest Verifications**

Then the Heavenly Worthy addressed the four assemblies, saying: The merits of this scripture can shatter the Iron Enclosure and all mountains, drain the waters of the Sea of Suffering, break open the great hells, and liberate all from sin and suffering. It subdues violent demons, protects all lands, annihilates all evil spirits, cures all grave illnesses, dissolves all poisons, severs ties with all wicked people, tames all venomous beasts, and overthrows all heterodox paths. All the heavens revere it, and its remaining merits are beyond enumeration.

Devout reverence for this scripture and the August Lord yields thirty kinds of merit.

Then the Heavenly Worthy again addressed the four assemblies, saying: The merits of this scripture can crush the Yin Feng and Iron Enclosure mountains, purifying all past defilements. It dries the waves of the Sea of Suffering, allowing one to turn back and ascend its shores. It shatters the great hells, stilling delusive conditions. It uproots all sin and suffering, severing karmic roots to forever end retribution. It subdues violent demons, restraining their fierce and malevolent perversity. It protects all lands, bringing purity and peace, enriching nations and securing the people. It annihilates all evil spirits, eradicating the dark and malevolent. It cures all grave illnesses, eliminating all defilements. It dissolves all poisons, dispelling worldly toxins and the great inner poisons of the body. It severs ties with all wicked people—either preventing encounters or causing them to flee at one’s sight. It tames all venomous beasts, pacifying the world’s poisonous creatures.

Moreover, those who cultivate the Dao—through the transformation of yin qi—command countless dragons, fierce beasts, giant serpents, and lions, each in the hundreds of millions, to guard this true scripture, rendering them docile and eternally protective.

It shatters all heterodox ways, crushing the world’s myriad deviant paths and demolishing one’s own deluded attachments. All the heavens—every realm’s celestial beings—naturally revere and honor this scripture. Its remaining virtues are beyond enumeration; as previously described, the merits of this scripture dissolve calamities and their transformations, eradicate disasters and their poisons, transform all without exception, and benefit all without limit. It is the great expedient, the supreme dharma among all teachings. Though uttered in the subtle words of the utmost sagely, it is the very function of one’s inherent nature. Strive diligently, and merit will naturally manifest.

**Chapter on Manifest Verification, Continuation of the Thirty-Sixth**

At that time, the assembly in the Dao altar—Golden Immortals, Bodhisattvas, and the retinue of Perfected Sages—having heard this teaching, rejoiced with exultation. They bowed their heads in reverence and offered this hymn of praise:

Great is the supreme Dao,
Peerless, the Most High Perfected.
Above, it delivers the heavens;
Below, it rescues the lost souls.
Without master or ancestor,
The Dao alone is its body.
Cinnabar Terrace and Purple Palace,
Golden Gates and Jade Capital—
Here is concealed this wondrous dharma,
Bestowing blessings upon all beings,
Erasing my ten thousand sins,
Prolonging my distant years.
Myriad spirits pay homage,
Demon kings guard and welcome.
Virtues flourish and prosper,
My name inscribed in the Yellow Register.
Through boundless eons,
May I endure forever.

When the assembly had finished reciting this hymn, they bowed their heads in homage, took their leave, and departed.

At that time, the assembly in the Dao altar—the place where the Dao is expounded—Golden Immortals, Bodhisattvas, and the retinue of Perfected Sages, having heard the scripture’s conclusion, rejoiced with exultation, their joy overflowing. They bowed their heads in reverence and offered this hymn:

Great is the supreme Dao,
Vast beyond measure,
Utmost and unattainable.
Peerless, the Most High Perfected,
Without origin or beginning,
The highest and most true.
Above, it delivers the heavens,
Its transformation pervading the heights.
Below, it rescues the lost souls,
Its transformation penetrating the nether darkness,
All lingering spirits ascending.
Without master or ancestor,
No teacher, no progenitor.
The Dao alone is its body—
In praising this scripture,
The Dao is its essence.
Cinnabar Terrace and Purple Palace,
Realm of the Great Mystery’s wonders.
Golden Gates and Jade Capital—
As previously described.
Here is concealed this wondrous dharma,
Secret and treasured.
Bestowing blessings upon all beings,
Or universally delivering all.
Erasing my ten thousand sins,
This scripture extinguishes all transgressions.
Prolonging my distant years,
This scripture extends life.
Myriad spirits pay homage,
Revering this scripture.
Demon kings guard and welcome
Those who uphold it.
Virtues flourish and prosper,
Vast and all-pervading, enduring and boundless.
My name inscribed in the Yellow Register,
Recorded in the immortal ledgers of the Mystic Capital,
On golden tablets and yellow registers.
Through boundless eons,
Vast and limitless, countless kalpas.
May those who uphold this scripture endure forever.

When the assembly of Perfected Ones had finished reciting this hymn, they bowed their heads in homage, took refuge in *The Supreme Jade Emperor’s Original Acts Sutra*, and departed from the presence of the Most High Sage.

**Thus concludes the lower scroll of *The Supreme Jade Emperor’s Original Acts Sutra*.**
